# Allergy season is starting 20 days earlier. That means the misery starts sooner.

![Pollen blankets a car windshield in a Massachusetts yard in June 2024.](https://bostonglobe-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/43AEARUHXQABG6Q7NHAHWMP644.jpg?auth=dad18ff2019b7152e80aa88eb2dcd0939f935f1d08d820403193d0086c205a1b&width=1440)

I’ve been coughing since early April. At least that’s how it feels. As someone who’s battled seasonal allergies my entire life, with a touch of asthma in the mix, I’m used to springtime discomfort.The sneezing and watery eyes are usually just the beginning with the release of tree pollen this time of year.

But this year seems different.

It began with what seemed like a standard upper respiratory infection. As symptoms persisted, I quickly found myself at an urgent care clinic, making subsequent calls to my physician.

My doctors cycled through treatments: first antibiotics, then decongestants, and finally allergy medications. Either I caught the most persistent cold imaginable or, somewhere along the way, spring allergies took over.

“There’s a real synergy between colds and allergies, especially if someone gets sick during tree pollen season. The result is often a longer, more intense period of symptoms,” said Dr. Frederic Little, a pulmonologist and allergist at Boston Medical Center.

Whether it was just allergies or a combination, I felt miserable.

Advertisement

Dry and windy days trigger the worst allergies, yet [last week’s rainy weather](https://www.bostonglobe.com/2025/05/07/metro/dave-epstein-new-england-weekend-forecast/ "https://www.bostonglobe.com/2025/05/07/metro/dave-epstein-new-england-weekend-forecast/") and the recent [wet weekends](https://www.bostonglobe.com/2025/04/11/metro/boston-new-england-rainy-weather/ "https://www.bostonglobe.com/2025/04/11/metro/boston-new-england-rainy-weather/"), though a nuisance for many, were a blessing for allergy sufferers by helping suppress the burgeoning pollen season. You might be wondering, then, if this season is relatively tame, why am I and others still suffering? That is a great question, and the answer lies in a longer allergy season.

Allergies have been starting weeks before the blooms begin here in New England. You might even start coughing and sneezing before the snow melts for the season.

Advertisement

“What’s been validated [in scientific research](https://www.pnas.org/doi/10.1073/pnas.2013284118 "https://www.pnas.org/doi/10.1073/pnas.2013284118") is that both the duration and intensity of pollen seasons have increased in temperate zones like where we live… climate change has shifted the baseline,” said Little.

[One study that examined 60 locations](https://www.pnas.org/doi/full/10.1073/pnas.2013284118 "https://www.pnas.org/doi/full/10.1073/pnas.2013284118") across North America found pollen seasons expanded by an average of 20 days from 1990 to 2018, and pollen concentrations increased by 21 percent.

The USA National Phenology Network’s [Spring Leaf Index Anomaly](https://www.usanpn.org/data/maps/spring) indicates that leaves have emerged about two weeks ahead of schedule in the Northeast.

![The spring leaf index for the United States this year.](https://bostonglobe-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/ND33LD2NE5DOZIUN677Y3UC7GU.jpeg?auth=19e377bae53ec72f2deada57b25feec97d30244ed0f47b19dd9350bdac9e79fb&width=1440)

Interestingly, Little explained, the pollen that descends upon New England starting as early as February often “isn’t even from here — it’s from trees in the Southeast.”

The pollen released from trees down South “can travel up to 30,000 feet and ride the jet stream north, arriving before our local species even bloom,” he said. Then, as high pressure and sinking air move in, those pollen particles find their way back down to the surface.

According to meteorologist Shel Winkley, the growing season has increased significantly across the Carolinas, which in turn kicks off pollen season even earlier.

“Raleigh’s growing season has increased by 38 days. Charlotte, Asheville, Greenville, all are seeing a month or more of extra plant growth time per year,” said Winkley. A longer season in the Carolinas translates into an earlier season here in New England.

Some experts believe there is another piece to the equation that’s worsening your symptoms: [carbon dioxide](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s00484-018-1558-7 "https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s00484-018-1558-7"). Research has shown that an increase in human-caused CO2 emissions is cranking out tree pollen grains [in greater numbers](https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s00484-018-1558-7 "https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s00484-018-1558-7").

Advertisement

“(Carbon dioxide) is plant food. It doesn’t just warm the planet — it supercharges plants to grow more and produce more pollen, making allergy seasons not only longer but more intense,” Winkley said. Atmospheric carbon dioxide levels have now surpassed 425 parts per million, which is the highest concentration in human history and a clear marker of accelerating climate change.

## **New England’s triggering pollens**

Trees, grass, and weeds are prolific producers of pollen, generating up to 1 billion pollen grains, according to the [Asthma and Allergy Foundation of America](https://urldefense.com/v3/__https://aafa.org/allergies/types-of-allergies/pollen-allergy/ragweed-pollen/__;!!BspMT6SJLSDJ!JcCiH25u64SC89EHyzQ7hTUFTdZm36qxdIZdTlsP1W7qbb5dbtwHx1AQMMsR5znc8iLch9PrhUQ8YFbZkCxgqnYyzXCqXA$). Tree pollens are quite potent and tend to cause significant symptoms. The pollen irritates the eyes, nose, skin, and throat, causing itchy, watery eyes, sneezing, and swollen sinuses.

Despite the longer allergy season, the foundation ranked Boston, Worcester, and Providence as “better than average” places to live with seasonal allergies, according to its [annual allergy report](https://aafa.org/asthma-allergy-research/allergy-capitals/ "https://aafa.org/asthma-allergy-research/allergy-capitals/") that examined data from the top 100 cities in the US.

Doctors agree that New England’s pollen levels are about the same as last year, “but if somebody is super allergic to certain deciduous tree pollens, they can feel a lot worse than the average individual. And with the growing season getting longer, even an average year can still feel pretty miserable for a lot of people,” Little said.

![Tree pollens are the biggest irritants across the region this month.](https://bostonglobe-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/ZCJ5ONAYEJB5XJWGWYBVNTDDI4.png?auth=1b4e4707cf8ca8c573dd5f4650374065c373ce088147c4e7260eb5cec173c4f1&width=1440)

Common tree pollen triggers in the spring include juniper, alder, oak, cottonwood, cedar, hickory, birch, and willow, among others. Weeds are mainly triggers from late August into early fall.

According to the asthma foundation, more than 90 million people in the US suffer from allergies.

Advertisement

[Many free apps](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/allergy-plus-by-pollen-com/id1556701665 "https://apps.apple.com/us/app/allergy-plus-by-pollen-com/id1556701665") provide real-time pollen counts to help allergy sufferers get ahead of a bad day. In addition, the National Allergy Bureau, run by the American Academy of Allergy, Asthma and Immunology, has a [network of approximately 50 pollen-counting locations](https://pollen.aaaai.org/#/ "https://pollen.aaaai.org/#/") across the country. The closest one to Boston is in Lebanon, N.H., operated by Dartmouth Hitchcock Medical Center.

Dr. Karen Hsu Blatman, Dartmouth Hitchcock Medical Center’s section chief of allergy and clinical immunology, said taking proactive treatment can help patients find relief when allergies strike. “We recommend people start nasal steroid sprays a month ahead of the season — even before symptoms start. If you wait, it’s harder to get symptoms under control," she said.

*Chris Gloninger is a meteorologist and a senior climate scientist at the Woods Hole Group.*

# Sleep Won’t Fix This Kind of Fatigue. Here’s What Will.

You might be a different kind of tired, and there's a fix for that.

By [Caitlin Carlson](/author/447905/caitlin-carlson/ "Caitlin Carlson")

C.J. Burton

Our product picks are editor-tested, expert-approved. We may earn a commission through links on our site. [Why Trust Us?](https://www.menshealth.com/technology-gear/a43807148/our-expertise-mens-health-product-reviews/)

**YOU GOT EIGHT** hours of sleep last night, you have a clean bill of health, and you’re on a [deload week](https://www.menshealth.com/fitness/a19546874/surprising-reason-you-need-to-take-a-recovery-day/) from the gym. Somehow, though, you’re *exhausted*. Turns out, there are actually several types of fatigue that could be getting you down, according to [Saundra Dalton-Smith](https://www.drdaltonsmith.com/), MD, an internal medicine physician and author of [*Sacred Rest*](https://www.amazon.com/Sacred-Rest-Recover-Energy-Restore/dp/1478921684?pd_rd_w=Ceoft&content-id=amzn1.sym.dcf559c6-d374-405e-a13e-133e852d81e1&pf_rd_p=dcf559c6-d374-405e-a13e-133e852d81e1&pf_rd_r=SD6ZVC4AQZQPV1XTNYBQ&pd_rd_wg=j2KZa&pd_rd_r=401de36d-8b09-415b-b3ed-0af38cd4e9a2&pd_rd_i=1478921684&psc=1&linkCode=sl1&tag=menshealth-auto-20&linkId=5c6626f8cb39ccb72b30598728f1da8d&language=en_US&ref_=as_li_ss_tl), who’s spent years researching the subject. “When someone says they're fatigued, my first question is what kind of tired are you?,” Dr. Dalton-Smith says, adding that answers may go beyond the usual suspects of mental and physical fatigue and include emotional, social, and/or sensory. And in order to bounce back, you need to know which one you’re dealing with.

Fatigue is multifaceted, agrees MH advisor [W. Christopher Winter,](https://www.wchriswinter.com/#/) MD, a sleep medicine and neurology expert. He even wrote a book—[*The Sleep Solution*](https://www.amazon.com/Sleep-Solution-Why-Your-Broken/dp/0399583610/?tag=menshealth-auto-20)—in which he provides a potential cause for fatigue for every letter of the alphabet. “Sleepiness is inadequate sleep or dysfunctional sleep,” he says. Fatigue is much harder to pin down.

Yet, understanding the root cause is what will help you figure out how to improve it, adds [James Clarke](https://staffportal.curtin.edu.au/staff/profile/view/james-clarke-f15fe8ed/), PhD, a psychology lecturer at the School of Population Health at Curtin University in Australia who has conducted [research](https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/S2212144724000048) on emotional fatigue in the workforce.

## So, What Kind of Tired Are *You*?

**DR. DALTON-SMITH** recommends first asking yourself how you’ve been using your energy over the past week. Maybe you used a bunch of emotional energy suppressing the urge to lose it when your direct report dropped the ball on an important project. Or maybe you used up your allotment of social energy entertaining your kids more than usual this week. “If there’s an area where you use energy, but you don’t have a plan on how you’re going to restore that area, that’s likely a place you develop a deficit in,” she says.

Clarke points out that it can be challenging to determine what type of fatigue you’re dealing with on your own, and suggests seeking guidance from a psychologist or your general practitioner if you’re struggling—especially since fatigue can also be a sign of underlying mental health concerns such as depression. Dr. Winter adds that other physical causes of fatigue could include thyroid issues or a hormonal imbalance. If those aren’t the case and you’re still having trouble locking in on what kind of fatigue you might have, you can also find [a quiz](https://www.restquiz.com/quiz/rest-quiz-test/) on Dr. Dalton-Smith’s website that guides you through some helpful questions.

## How to Reclaim Your Energy

**ONCE YOU ID** the cause, counterintuitively, the ways to restore yourself aren’t always about doing less. “We have a misconception in our culture that, ‘oh, I'll take a vacation or I'll do a sabbatical,’” Dr. Dalton-Smith says. “To actually be a burnout prevention strategy, we need to build rest into routine practices so that there are small things that you do that have a big impact.” And it’s worth pointing out that logging your seven to nine hours of sleep at night and following other well-being best practices like eating well and exercising regularly is going to set you up to better deal with *any* type of fatigue.   
  
To get you started, we break down three non-physical types of fatigue that people often overlook—and reveal how to get the kind of rest you really need to feel vital and energized.

Advertisement - Continue Reading Below

## Emotional Fatigue

**What it is:** “When we talk about emotional exhaustion from the point of view of burnout, it's a very specific type of depletion,” Clarke says. “People will say they just feel like their emotional resources are used up, they may have more difficulty engaging with other peoples' emotions, or regulating their own, but they can still have energy to do other things, like engage in activities they like to do.”

Dr. Dalton-Smith adds that men with people-pleasing tendencies may be particularly susceptible to emotional fatigue. While this may be more often culturally associated with women, many men are people-pleasers, too, especially when it comes to work, which Dr. Dalton-Smith calls professional emotional labor. “In other words, you are suppressing your true emotions for the sake of staying professional in whatever that situation may be,” she says.

Dr. Dalton-Smith also sees people getting emotionally fatigued when they avoid exploring their true wants and needs. Maybe they’re in an unfulfilling job but feel stuck because of the time they’ve invested in their career. “This adds to a sense of shunted emotions, which then results in decreased joy, decreased satisfaction, sometimes depression, and other symptoms that are related to that,” she says.

**How to solve it:** [Practicing compassion](https://www.menshealth.com/health/a39982367/global-happiness-how-to-be-happier/) (for yourself and others) is one research-backed way to win back some emotional energy. “We know that people who have higher levels of self-compassion tend to have more healthy emotion regulation tendencies and tend to experience less emotional exhaustion,” Clarke says. “Compassion and self-compassion help give a direction for these feelings so we're less burdened by them.” Compassion generally means reminding yourself that some situations are stressful, that you’re human, and it involves figuring out how you can apply what you learned to future situations.

## Social Fatigue

**What it is:** “Most of the people we spend time with are negatively pulling from our social energy, meaning they have demands upon us, they need things from us,” she says, but simultaneously, they can *give*you energy. This can include friends, your spouse or partner, and even your children. Dr. Dalton-Smith recommends recognizing how your interactions affect your energy and ensuring that relationships don’t become one-sided—as in, it’s all pull and no pour.  **How to solve it:** Think about the people in your life that you enjoy being around, and make an effort to spend more time with those people, Dr. Dalton-Smith says. And while cutting out the draining people is often not possible, simply being *aware* that they’re draining—and that you may be more susceptible to social fatigue when you’re around them—can be helpful because you can then seek out social rest, specifically.

When Dr. Dalton-Smith herself needs social rest, she turns to a group text thread with two close friends. “I recently came back from a speaking tour in South Africa, and I had a moment,” she says. So she texted them and they both jumped in and said something that made her feel seen and appreciated—and restored in this domain.

If you’re partnered, make sure that in addition to the transactional conversations like scheduling and bills, you’re taking the time to talk about *life*, Dr. Dalton-Smith says, which could include celebrating even small milestones together or talking about what you both want for your future. Dr. Winter adds that it can be helpful to understand your partner’s capacity for social fatigue as well as your own. (Pro tip: Sending them a link to this article and suggesting a discussion may earn you quite a few EQ—emotional intelligence—points!)

Advertisement - Continue Reading Below

## Sensory Fatigue

**What it is:** “A lot of us work or live in noise pollution or very sensory-rich environments, and we're not cognitively aware of the amount of energy that is used just to process that information,” says Dr. Dalton-Smith. “Because even if you think that you are tuning it out, your brain is actively processing it, which leads to fatigue in that part of our system.” Signs of a sensory rest deficit include feeling particularly anxious at work or in other highly-sensory environments, or being “jumpy” when you hear your phone buzz, for example. People with ADHD or neurodivergency may be particularly susceptible to this type of fatigue, Dr. Dalton-Smith says.

**How to solve it:** “The correction is having specific ways of downgrading sensory input, whether that's using noise-cancellation earphones periodically throughout the day just to give yourself a moment of reprieve or having screen-free time or turning off the notifications on your phone,” Dr. Dalton-Smith says.

## When to See a Doctor

**EVERYONE GETS SLEEPY** and everyone experiences the above types of fatigue from time to time—it’s all perfectly normal, Dr. Winter says. “It's when people don't feel like there’s a reasonable explanation for their fatigue, that’s where we start to worry about these individuals.” Dr. Winter says if you've been struggling with overwhelming fatigue for more than a few weeks, talk to your primary care doctor, who may recommend blood work and hormone testing. If they give you the all-clear and you’re still struggling, see a sleep specialist who may be able to help you pinpoint other underlying causes of your tiredness.

[Caitlin Carlson](/author/447905/caitlin-carlson/)

Freelance writer

Caitlin is a health and fitness journalist based in New York City. She writes for publications including *The Wall Street Journal* and *Runner’s World.* She's completed 12 marathons, including the six World Marathon Majors, is semi-fluent in French, and volunteers as a greeter on The High Line. # Struggling With Brain Fog And Fatigue? You Might Be Lacking This 1 Essential Mineral.

Treating the issue could help you feel much better, but it may take some self-advocacy.

By [Jillian Wilson

Senior Wellness Reporter, HuffPost](https://www.huffpost.com/author/jillian-wilson)

LOADINGERROR LOADING

What if your exhaustion wasn’t just because of family stress, work tasks and social obligations? While those things can certainly cause fatigue, it turns out iron deficiency ― [which is present in roughly one-third of women](https://www.ama-assn.org/delivering-care/prevention-wellness/what-doctors-wish-patients-knew-about-iron-deficiency) who get a period ― can be the culprit.

“Many people think [iron is] just another vitamin, like you just didn’t take your iron, or you didn’t get enough in your diet, but it’s totally not that. Iron is a very important mineral ... that’s involved with every cell in the body utilizing energy,” said [Dr. Steven Fein](https://hemeoncall.com/meet-the-doctor/), a hematologist and owner of [HemeOnCall](https://hemeoncall.com/heme-on-call/), women’s health centers that treat iron deficiency, abnormal blood counts and more hematology issues.

Advertisement

“Your muscles cannot contract without iron. Your brain cannot think without iron,” he explained.

The issue is most prevalent in premenopausal women. “We think that about 30 million U.S. women have iron deficiency,” Fein said.

Iron deficiency can cause a host of issues, including a condition called iron deficiency anemia. “You can imagine it like a spectrum where iron deficiency without anemia is the milder version, and then if you get to a point where you have iron deficiency anemia ... if you get to that point where you’re that severe, then the symptoms are all the worse — more fatigue, more tiredness,” Fein said.

About 15% of American women have iron deficiency anemia, and another 15 or 20% have iron deficiency without anemia, according to Fein.

Advertisement

“Anemia ... means that the iron is low enough that the bone marrow has essentially failed to keep up. It needs iron to make red blood cells, and it just can’t make enough because it doesn’t have the right supplies,” explained [Dr. Joseph Shatzel](https://www.ohsu.edu/people/joseph-shatzel-md-mcr), a classical hematologist and associate professor in the school of medicine at Oregon Health and Science University.

Neither iron deficiency or iron deficiency anemia should be ignored, as they both can cause health problems. Both can be diagnosed via blood tests ordered by your doctor.

But getting diagnosed may take some self-advocating. “We do not have a routine recommendation in the U.S. to screen for iron deficiency,” Shatzel said. As a result, the problem often goes unaddressed.

Advertisement

Here’s what to know about iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia, including the signs you should bring up with your doctor:

## **Fatigue and brain fog are frequently reported symptoms of iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia.**

Women are often saddled with [the mental load](https://www.huffpost.com/entry/mom-mental-load_l_63f7a67ee4b0616708e04d9a) when it comes to caring for children, partners, parents and completing must-do tasks around the home. This is often associated with more fatigue and lower mood. And while that is certainly true, iron deficiency can play a role here as well.

Advertisement

The most common symptom of iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia is fatigue, “but difficulty concentrating, or poor concentration, that sort of mental fog ... is well noted,” Shatzel explained.

Signs of iron deficiency also include impaired memory and mood-related complications, Fein added. [Research shows](https://medicine.umich.edu/dept/psychiatry/news/archive/202305/could-low-iron-be-making-your-mental-health-symptoms-worse) that low iron can worsen [depression](https://www.huffpost.com/life/topic/depression) and anxiety, too. People may also have trouble catching their breath after exercise or going up stairs, according to Fein. It may also cause [you to feel dizzy or lightheaded](https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/22824-iron-deficiency-anemia).

“Sometimes, people have weird cravings like chewing ice or craving ice,” said Fein, who noted that restless leg syndrome is also reported. Hair thinning is another indicator, according to Shatzel.

Advertisement

## **Iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia are common in people who menstruate because of the blood loss.**

“Every time you have a menstrual cycle ... you lose blood. Blood is really your main store of iron,” said Shatzel, noting that it only takes a small amount of blood loss to spark the problem.

Advertisement

The body absorbs iron very slowly, and this is intentional “because if you do get excessive iron, that can be a health risk as well,” Shatzel explained.

“Probably about half of the women who have low iron have heavy periods that they don’t even realize a lot of the time,” Fein said.

There are also other causes of iron deficiency, including inflammatory bowel disease and Crohn’s disease, Fein noted. The problem can also be a sign of colon cancer, a gastric ulcer or even Celiac disease, according to Shatzel. These issues can happen in both men and women, but in men, the underlying cause of iron deficiency is [often more severe](https://www.ama-assn.org/delivering-care/prevention-wellness/what-doctors-wish-patients-knew-about-iron-deficiency).

Advertisement

There’s also been a rise in people getting gastric bypass weight loss surgery, “which causes iron deficiency on purpose by causing malabsorption of all nutrients,” Fein said.

But it’s largely an issue among women with periods and bleeding disorders, Fein added.

## **Iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia is common in pregnancy and can cause complications.**

Iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia is also common (and under-diagnosed) in pregnant people, according to both experts, which can be particularly dangerous.

[Research shows](https://pmc.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/articles/PMC9541841/) that iron deficiency can cause complications in pregnancy for both the mother and the baby, Shatzel noted. These include complications like preterm birth, low birth weight and [developmental delays](https://www.nhlbi.nih.gov/health/anemia/pregnancy). If moms are fatigued already from low iron, they’re less able to push, resulting in more C-sections, Fein said. [C-sections are more risky](https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/treatments/7246-cesarean-birth-c-section) than vaginal delivery.

Advertisement

“And this is a public health problem that affects Black people disproportionately, because it turns out that half of [pregnant] Black people have iron deficiency, and a third of non-Black [pregnant] people have iron deficiency,” Fein added.

## **Treating low iron can improve quality of life.**

Getting iron levels to a healthy range not only brings your body back to where it should be, but can make life more enjoyable, too.

Advertisement

Treating iron deficiency is done in one of two ways, either by oral iron pills or IV therapy, Shatzel explained. The best remedy depends on the person. Your doctor can help you get the right treatment, but experts say IV iron often tends to be more effective.

If left untreated, in rare cases, blood transfusions are necessary, Shatzel said.

It’s also important to treat the underlying cause of iron deficiency, which for many women is heavy periods, and can benefit from birth control and other medical interventions, according to Shatzel. But since low iron can also be caused by GI issues, GI workups are sometimes necessary to figure out the best treatment plan.

“I think the biggest thing in the general population is the quality of life. It’s pretty clear people feel better when they’re not anemic and their iron is at a good level,” Shatzel said.

Advertisement

Iron deficiency can make folks tired, unfocused and anxious, which impedes day-to-day functioning, whether that’s spending time with loved ones, going to work or heading out for a hike.

[With normal iron levels, athletic performance will likely improve](https://pmc.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/articles/PMC10608302/), making that run, dance class or HIIT class a little less tiring. Or you may find you have enough energy for better performance at work, said Fein, as heavy periods, tiredness and brain fog can result in missed work days and trouble concentrating on tasks.

“At the very least, it’s a quality of life issue for all these women,” Fein said. “And not only that, it’s a gender inequality issue to the point [where] a woman may not be able to function well at work. They may not get the job promotion or the salary that they deserve because they have this [issue], whereas men do not have this problem.”

Advertisement

“My general sense of this is that it hasn’t really been as important as it should be to the medical community because this is a very common thing that the majority of people suffering from are women,” Shatzel said.

If you get a period and suffer from brain fog, fatigue or any of the symptoms associated with iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia, it’s worth talking to your doctor about potential testing. It may be the step you need to take to start living a more enjoyable life.

Signs of iron deficiency also include impaired memory and mood-related complications, Fein added. [Research shows](https://medicine.umich.edu/dept/psychiatry/news/archive/202305/could-low-iron-be-making-your-mental-health-symptoms-worse) that low iron can worsen [depression](https://www.huffpost.com/life/topic/depression) and anxiety, too. People may also have trouble catching their breath after exercise or going up stairs, according to Fein. It may also cause [you to feel dizzy or lightheaded](https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/22824-iron-deficiency-anemia).

“Sometimes, people have weird cravings like chewing ice or craving ice,” said Fein, who noted that restless leg syndrome is also reported. Hair thinning is another indicator, according to Shatzel.

Advertisement

## **Iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia are common in people who menstruate because of the blood loss.**

“Every time you have a menstrual cycle ... you lose blood. Blood is really your main store of iron,” said Shatzel, noting that it only takes a small amount of blood loss to spark the problem.

Advertisement

The body absorbs iron very slowly, and this is intentional “because if you do get excessive iron, that can be a health risk as well,” Shatzel explained.

“Probably about half of the women who have low iron have heavy periods that they don’t even realize a lot of the time,” Fein said.

There are also other causes of iron deficiency, including inflammatory bowel disease and Crohn’s disease, Fein noted. The problem can also be a sign of colon cancer, a gastric ulcer or even Celiac disease, according to Shatzel. These issues can happen in both men and women, but in men, the underlying cause of iron deficiency is [often more severe](https://www.ama-assn.org/delivering-care/prevention-wellness/what-doctors-wish-patients-knew-about-iron-deficiency).

Advertisement

There’s also been a rise in people getting gastric bypass weight loss surgery, “which causes iron deficiency on purpose by causing malabsorption of all nutrients,” Fein said.

But it’s largely an issue among women with periods and bleeding disorders, Fein added.

## **Iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia is common in pregnancy and can cause complications.**

Iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia is also common (and under-diagnosed) in pregnant people, according to both experts, which can be particularly dangerous.

[Research shows](https://pmc.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/articles/PMC9541841/) that iron deficiency can cause complications in pregnancy for both the mother and the baby, Shatzel noted. These include complications like preterm birth, low birth weight and [developmental delays](https://www.nhlbi.nih.gov/health/anemia/pregnancy). If moms are fatigued already from low iron, they’re less able to push, resulting in more C-sections, Fein said. [C-sections are more risky](https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/treatments/7246-cesarean-birth-c-section) than vaginal delivery.

Advertisement

“And this is a public health problem that affects Black people disproportionately, because it turns out that half of [pregnant] Black people have iron deficiency, and a third of non-Black [pregnant] people have iron deficiency,” Fein added.

## **Treating low iron can improve quality of life.**

Getting iron levels to a healthy range not only brings your body back to where it should be, but can make life more enjoyable, too.

Advertisement

Treating iron deficiency is done in one of two ways, either by oral iron pills or IV therapy, Shatzel explained. The best remedy depends on the person. Your doctor can help you get the right treatment, but experts say IV iron often tends to be more effective.

If left untreated, in rare cases, blood transfusions are necessary, Shatzel said.

It’s also important to treat the underlying cause of iron deficiency, which for many women is heavy periods, and can benefit from birth control and other medical interventions, according to Shatzel. But since low iron can also be caused by GI issues, GI workups are sometimes necessary to figure out the best treatment plan.

“I think the biggest thing in the general population is the quality of life. It’s pretty clear people feel better when they’re not anemic and their iron is at a good level,” Shatzel said.

Advertisement

Iron deficiency can make folks tired, unfocused and anxious, which impedes day-to-day functioning, whether that’s spending time with loved ones, going to work or heading out for a hike.

[With normal iron levels, athletic performance will likely improve](https://pmc.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/articles/PMC10608302/), making that run, dance class or HIIT class a little less tiring. Or you may find you have enough energy for better performance at work, said Fein, as heavy periods, tiredness and brain fog can result in missed work days and trouble concentrating on tasks.

“At the very least, it’s a quality of life issue for all these women,” Fein said. “And not only that, it’s a gender inequality issue to the point [where] a woman may not be able to function well at work. They may not get the job promotion or the salary that they deserve because they have this [issue], whereas men do not have this problem.”

Advertisement

“My general sense of this is that it hasn’t really been as important as it should be to the medical community because this is a very common thing that the majority of people suffering from are women,” Shatzel said.

If you get a period and suffer from brain fog, fatigue or any of the symptoms associated with iron deficiency and iron deficiency anemia, it’s worth talking to your doctor about potential testing. It may be the step you need to take to start living a more enjoyable life.

# Subtle signs on your skin and neck that mean you could have deadly condition suffered by 100m

By [ISHITA SRIVASTAVA FOR DAILYMAIL.COM](/profile-2841/ishita-srivastava.html)

Published:  11:42 EDT, 28 May 2025   |  Updated:  12:21 EDT, 28 May 2025

13

View   
 comments

Unexplained changes in your skin can occur for a number of reasons - whether it's from time in the sun or allergies. However, a health coach warns they could be a sign of something more sinister.

Jade Rivers, a wellness coach, recently revealed 'what a body looks like when it's heading toward [type 2] diabetes.'

Type 2 diabetes is the most common form of the condition globally and over 37million American adults suffer from this form of the chronic illness.

It is caused by [either the pancreas not producing enough insulin](/health/article-11238421/Even-SLIM-type-2-diabetics-reverse-condition.html) or the body's cells not responding properly to insulin. This leads to high blood sugar levels and a buildup of glucose in the bloodstream, which can damage the eyes, kidneys, nerves and heart.

It is often linked to lifestyle factors like obesity, poor diet and lack of physical activity and because it develops gradually, people may not know they have it until serious complications arise.

However, according to Rivers, if people are able to recognize several changes in their bodies that indicate insulin resistance - a precursor to diabetes that plagues 100million people - they may be able to make changes and reverse it.

Below, DailyMail.com details the unexpected signs you could be headed toward a type 2 diabetes diagnosis: 

## Dark patches on the neck and underarms

![Insulin resistance can lead to the build of the hormone in the body, which can cause dark spots and rashes on the skin](https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2025/05/28/16/98830083-14740755-image-a-58_1748446108253.jpg)

Insulin resistance can lead to the build of the hormone in the body, which can cause dark spots and rashes on the skin

Dark, velvety patches on the skin, often in body folds like the neck and armpits, can be a sign of acanthosis nigricans (AN).

This is a skin condition often associated with obesity and insulin resistance, and a possible early sign of type 2 diabetes.

The patches are not caused by diabetes itself, but rather by the underlying insulin resistance.

#### Read More

#### Type 2 diabetics can add over a DECADE to their lives through simple lifestyle changes such as slimming down to a healthy weight, study finds

![article image](https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2022/04/18/20/56756925-0-image-a-29_1650310473664.jpg)

AN is characterized by dark, velvety patches in areas across the body like the neck, armpits, groin, and sometimes on the hands, elbows, or knees.

It is typically a sign your body is making extra insulin. When the body is resistant to insulin, the pancreas may overproduce the hormone in order to compensate.

This excess insulin then builds up and causes the dark patches.

While it can cause embarrassment and some people may try to scrub or bleach the patches away, this is not effective in getting rid of the dark spots.

Instead, you should change your diet to include more healthy foods and get physical activity. Losing weight can also help. This will lower the amount of excess insulin in the body and can alleviate AN.

Skin tags

Skin tags, also known as acrochordons, are small, harmless growths often found in areas where skin folds or rubs together, such as the neck, armpits and groin.

They may also appear where skin rubs against clothing or jewelry and are caused by friction.

While typically benign, if you begin noticing the appearance of more skin tags than is normal for you, a trip to the doctor may be in order.

![Jade Rivers, a wellness expert, who noted that dark patches on the neck and underarms and a slight hump on at the neck are all signs that your body is heading towards Type 2 diabetes](https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2025/05/28/16/98666699-14740755-Jade_Rivers_a_wellness_expert_who_noted_that_dark_patches_on_the-a-69_1748446843885.jpg)

Jade Rivers, a wellness expert, who noted that dark patches on the neck and underarms and a slight hump on at the neck are all signs that your body is heading towards Type 2 diabetes

In people with insulin resistance, skin tags form because insulin plays a role in regulating cell growth.

When someone is insulin resistant and the pancreas produces too much, it can stimulate the growth of skin cells, which in turn can lead to skin tags.

Additionally, insulin resistance can disrupt the balance of the hormone insulin-growth factor-1 (IGF-1), which is linked to skin tag formation.

A hump or fat around your neck Neck

A neck hump, sometimes called a buffalo hump, is a fat pad that forms at the base of the back of the neck.

Being insulin resistant and struggling with a build up of insulin in the body leads to weight gain, fat accumulation and a struggle to lose weight.

This could cause fat deposits to collect in certain areas of the body, such as the neck.

Additionally, the hormone imbalance caused by insulin resistance or full-blown diabetes contributes to abnormal fat distribution.

Like many other symptoms of insulin resistance, a hump or fat around the neck can be alleviated by diet and exercise changes, which can lead to healthy weight loss.

Is eating once a day a good idea? Experts share varying opinions on the ‘OMAD diet’
===================================================================================

A form of intermittent fasting, the OMAD diet could be beneficial for some, but risks exist
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By [Eve Glover](https://www.foxnews.com/person/g/eve-glover) [Fox News](https://www.foxnews.com/)

Published December 11, 2024 4:30am EST

[Having trouble? Click here.](https://help.foxnews.com/hc/en-us/articles/23074352680475-Are-you-encountering-any-technical-challenges-while-trying-to-log-into-Fox-News-to-access-special-content)

Traditional guidance has been to eat [three square meals](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/nutrition-and-fitness/nutrition) a day — but a trending diet plan has some people eating just once.

Dubbed the One Meal a Day (OMAD) diet, it’s a form of intermittent fasting that involves eating all the d[ay’s calories](https://www.foxnews.com/category/food-drink/food) in a single meal, after 23 hours of fasting.

Dr. Jason Fung, a Canadian nephrologist (kidney specialist), is known to be an expert in intermittent fasting (IF). He spoke with Fox News Digital about the OMAD diet, which he described as a stricter version of IF.

[**'I'M A HEART SURGEON, HERE'S WHAT YOU SHOULD KNOW ABOUT EGGS, YOUR HEART AND YOUR HEALTH'**](https://www.foxnews.com/food-drink/im-heart-surgeon-heres-should-know-eggs-heart-health)

Both diets involve "time-restricted eating," Fung noted — but with intermittent fasting, people can eat twice a day.

If you only eat once a day, the natural tendency will be to eat less overall, he said.

 ![Image 2: Woman eating steak](https://a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2024/12/1200/675/woman-eating-steak-salad.jpg?ve=1&tl=1)

The One Meal a Day (OMAD) diet is a form of intermittent fasting that involves eating all of the day’s calories in a single meal, after 23 hours of fasting.  (iStock)

The body is either in a state of storing calories or burning them, according to the expert.

When a person fasts for an extended period, the body begins to use fat for energy, which can actually decrease hunger, Fung said.

**Who could benefit?**
----------------------

The two main health conditions that can greatly benefit from OMAD and intermittent fasting are weight loss and [type 2 diabetes](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/diabetes/diabetes-type-2), according to Fung.

"Fasting really impacts weight and sugars, because that's the way calories are stored – as sugar and fat," he said.

[**FASTING-LIKE DIET COULD SLOW THE AGING PROCESS, STUDY SUGGESTS: ‘LIVING LONGER AND HEALTHIER’**](https://www.foxnews.com/health/fasting-like-diet-could-slow-aging-process-study-living-longer-and-healthier)

Losing weight can potentially reduce the risk of heart disease, stroke and obesity-related cancers, the doctor noted, in addition to alleviating back pain, knee pain and pressure on joints.

"You can actually reverse your [type 2 diabetes](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/diabetes) with intermittent fasting," Fung said, referencing previously studies published by the National Institutes of Health and Diabetes Care.

 ![Image 3: Time-restricted eating](https://a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2023/12/1200/675/time-restricted-eating.jpg?ve=1&tl=1)

When a person fasts for an extended period, the body begins to use fat for energy, which can actually decrease hunger, one expert said.  (iStock)

Fung described how one of his patients who had diabetes for 15 years was able to discontinue his insulin medication after going on the OMAD diet three times a week for a month.

The patient is still not taking insulin and continues to fast regularly, though not as frequently, he added.

> "You can actually reverse your type 2 diabetes with intermittent fasting."

People with hypoglycemia who are not on blood glucose-lowering type 2 diabetes medications should still be able to [follow the OMAD diet](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/nutrition-and-fitness/diet-trends) if they avoid highly refined carbohydrates, which can cause glucose levels to spike, said Fung.

He recommends eating whole, natural, [unprocessed foods](https://www.foxnews.com/category/food-drink/food/healthy-foods).

 ![Image 4: Food timing - fasting](https://a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2023/09/1200/675/food-timing-fasting.jpg?ve=1&tl=1)

"Fasting really impacts weight and sugars, because that's the way calories are stored – as sugar and fat," one fasting expert told Fox News Digital. (iStock)

Fern Katzman, a Toronto-based clinical nutritionist, told Fox News Digital that she has seen patients with type 2 diabetes go off Metformin, an [oral antidiabetic medication](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/healthy-living/medications), or not have to go on it at all after engaging in intermittent fasting, or OMAD.

Katzman said people should have a reason to go on OMAD, such as to address medical issues or to bring down elevated blood sugar levels after a period of eating or drinking excessively.

[**HIDDEN BELLY FAT COULD SIGNAL ALZHEIMER’S DISEASE RISK 15 YEARS BEFORE SYMPTOMS SHOW UP, STUDY FINDS**](https://www.foxnews.com/health/hidden-belly-fat-could-signal-alzheimers-disease-risk-15-years-symptoms-study-finds)

"Insulin drives cravings," she told Fox News Digital. "After you eat or drink a lot, your insulin spikes, and that makes you hungry."

Katzman added, "The one thing that everybody tells me when they've done OMAD is that the cravings stop — and that is the key to any [weight loss program](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/nutrition-and-fitness/weight-loss)."

 ![Image 5: Woman checking blood sugar](https://a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2024/07/1200/675/woman-checking-diabetes.jpg?ve=1&tl=1)

The two main health conditions that can greatly benefit from OMAD and intermittent fasting are weight loss and type 2 diabetes, an expert said. (iStock)

In addition to losing weight, Katzman said her patients have reported [better digestion](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/digestive-health) and decreased bloating on the OMAD diet because "sugar makes yeast and yeast bloats you."

Patients have also noticed immediate improvements in their mood and energy levels on the diet, she added.

Katzman recommends filling up on vegetables, protein and grains, like quinoa and small amounts of brown rice.

**‘Not for everyone’**
----------------------

Katzman cautioned that OMAD is "not for everyone" — it’s likely not a good choice for those who have eating disorders or are hypoglycemic, for example.

[**CLICK HERE TO GET THE FOX NEWS APP**](https://www.foxnews.com/apps-products?pid=AppArticleLink)

Dr. Lisa Young, a registered dietitian nutritionist in Florida, echoed those same concerns, warning that the OMAD diet can trigger people with [eating disorders](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/mental-health/eating-disorders).

"You're not focusing on your intuitive internal signals of hunger and fullness," she told Fox News Digital. "You're not trusting yourself."

 ![Image 6: Healthy whole foods](https://a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2024/12/1200/675/healthy-whole-foods.jpg?ve=1&tl=1)

For those following the diet, experts recommend sticking to "whole, natural, unprocessed foods." (iStock)

Young also warned that the diet can "make you fatigued."

"It could even make you hungrier and cause hypoglycemia (low blood sugar)," she added.

[**CLICK HERE TO SIGN UP FOR OUR HEALTH NEWSLETTER**](https://www.foxnews.com/newsletters?cmpid=fnfirstnl)

Dr. Joel Kahn, a [holistic cardiologist](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/heart-health) in Michigan, is also not a proponent of the OMAD diet.

The doctor noted that studies from the National Institutes of Health and the Journal of the American Medical Association (JAMA) substantiate that eating just one meal in the evening can result in declining metabolic health, higher blood sugar levels and greater insulin resistance.

> "You're not focusing on your intuitive internal signals of hunger and fullness."

"Theoretically, if you're going to do a One Meal a Day diet, you might actually do it in the morning hours," Kahn told Fox News Digital.

[_**For more Health articles, visit**_](https://www.foxnews.com/health) [_**www.foxnews.com/health**_](http://www.foxnews.com/health)

The doctor instead recommends the Daniel Diet, which he described as a "faith-based diet" of plants and legumes inspired by the Book of Daniel.

Khan is also a fan of the Prolon 5-Day Program, a plant-based [fasting-mimicking diet](https://www.foxnews.com/category/health/nutrition-and-fitness), which he said could help people achieve a younger biological age.

Eve Glover is a contributing writer for Fox News Digital.

# ‘Late dinners, 1 on 10’: As a nutritionist rates daily practices for diabetes, find out what truly helps control sugar levels

## Are you making these mistakes as a diabetic?

By: [Lifestyle Desk](/agency/lifestyle-desk/) 
  
New Delhi | Updated: September 2, 2025 03:28 PM IST

4 min read

Some daily habits may be harmful to those with diabetes (Source: Freepik)

Managing diabetes often comes down to everyday choices, and even small lifestyle habits can make a big difference in controlling blood sugar levels. 

Nutritionist and content creator Deepsikha Jain recently shared her perspective by rating common daily practices for those with diabetes. She explained, “Let’s rate these **[habits for diabetes](https://indianexpress.com/article/lifestyle/life-style/2-simple-habits-diabetics-manage-blood-sugar-experts-9313624/)** as a nutritionist. Fruits on an empty stomach, 2 on 10, this can cause a sugar spike. Not good for those who have diabetes. Fat first, empty stomach, 10 on 10, it will help balance your blood sugar.”

She continued, “Veggies before meals, 9 on 10. This will help slow down the absorption of glucose and not cause a sugar spike. Late dinners, 1 on 10. This can cause a sugar spike, also increasing your cortisol level. Walking after meals, 10 on 10, will help reduce sugar spikes by 30%. So share this with all the people who have diabetes.”

Story continues below this ad

While her breakdown provides a quick reference for those looking to adjust their eating habits and daily routine, it also sparks questions about the science behind these ratings.

## **Fruits on an empty stomach**

Kanikka Malhotra, a certified diabetes educator, tells [indianexpress.com](https://indianexpress.com), “For people with diabetes, eating fruit on an empty stomach can cause sharper blood sugar rises, mainly because fruit sugars absorb quickly when nothing slows them down. However, fruit is an important part of a healthy diet and need not be feared. The key is pairing fruit with protein or healthy fats, which helps your body absorb sugars more gradually. Choose whole, fibre-rich fruits like berries, apples, or pears, and regulate portions. Avoid fruit juices and canned fruits in syrup as they spike sugar rapidly. Remember, managing diabetes isn’t about avoiding fruit, but eating it wisely and as part of a balanced meal.”

## **Fat first, empty stomach**

Malhotra states, “Scientifically speaking, fat delays gastric emptying, which can blunt the initial blood sugar spike after a meal. However, high-fat meals lead to delayed, prolonged rises in blood sugar and increased insulin needs, especially in people with type 1 diabetes. This is partly because free fatty acids from fat cause insulin resistance and stimulate hepatic glucose production over several hours. There is also risk of excess calorie intake and worsening cardiovascular health with too much saturated fat.” 

Thus, “fat first” is not a universal fix. The safest, evidence-based approach is a balanced meal with healthy fats, fiber, and lean protein instead of isolated fat consumption. 

Story continues below this ad

## **On walking after meals**

Taking a simple walk after eating is one of the most effective and practical tools to manage blood sugar. Malhotra explains that [**walking for just 10 minutes after a meal**](https://indianexpress.com/article/lifestyle/health-specials/post-meal-walk-blood-sugar-study-8074135/) can significantly reduce post-meal glucose spikes and help maintain better long-term control. Even shorter walks, of 2-5 minutes, are valuable if done consistently.

## **Veggies before meals vs late dinners**

Malhotra confirms that eating non-starchy veggies—like salad or sautéed greens—before the main part of a meal “is scientifically proven to tame post-meal sugar spikes.” Veggies provide fiber, which acts as a barrier and slows down how quickly sugars from the rest of the meal hit the bloodstream. 

“Late dinners, on the other hand, disturb the body’s clock. Insulin sensitivity drops at night, so late eating leads to higher sugar and cortisol levels overnight. Over time, this pattern increases the risk of poor control and complications. Choose early dinners and prioritise veggies for steadier blood sugars and overall metabolic health,” concludes Malhotra.

Follow Us
0- آخرین تحقیقات دربارهٔ سرطان سینه چه یافته‌هایی داشته‌اند؟: Recent research on breast cancer has yielded several important findings. A study published in Radiology revealed that rates of late-stage breast cancer at diagnosis have increased among women of all racial and ethnic groups, with Black women being the most affected. The sharpest increases were observed in young women aged 20 to 39 and women over 75. In the realm of detection, artificial intelligence has shown promise in improving breast cancer screening. A retrospective study found that AI assistance in mammography screening can detect more cases of false negatives and cancers with minimal signs. Additionally, a simulation study reported increased breast cancer detection and reduced radiologist workload when AI-based triaging was used in mammography screening. Machine learning approaches, including deep learning and radiomics, have demonstrated superior performance in classifying breast cancer using radiological imaging and histopathological slides. Advanced ensemble learning algorithms like Gradient Boosted Trees and XGBoost have been effectively employed to predict metastasis and survival outcomes in breast cancer patients.
0- بهترین اقدامات اولیه برای مشکوک به سکته مغزی چیست ؟: The most important initial actions for a suspected stroke are to act quickly and call emergency medical services immediately. The acronym BEFAST can help identify stroke symptoms: Balance changes, Eyesight problems, Facial drooping, Arm weakness, Speech difficulties, and Time to call for help. It's crucial not to ignore or downplay these symptoms, as a warning stroke is considered an emergency. Upon arrival at the hospital, clearly communicate to medical staff that you suspect a stroke to ensure prompt treatment. Do not wait for symptoms to resolve on their own, as they may not. Instead, go to the nearest emergency room as soon as possible if you experience any sudden onset of these signs. Quick action and proper communication with healthcare providers are essential for the best possible outcome in cases of suspected stroke.
0- آیا قرص ملاتونین برای بی‌خوابی طولانی‌مدت بی‌خطر است؟: The long-term safety of melatonin for chronic insomnia is not fully established. While melatonin is generally considered safer than other sleep medications, prolonged daily use may have potential negative implications. Experts suggest it's typically intended for short-term use of several weeks or months rather than continuous long-term use. Although melatonin isn't known to cause dependency, taking breaks from it periodically is recommended unless under a doctor's supervision. Some individuals may experience side effects like nausea or low energy, possibly due to metabolic or genetic factors. Higher doses can increase the likelihood of next-day grogginess. There's also concern that long-term use might disrupt the body's natural melatonin production, though research on this remains inconclusive. For chronic insomnia, it's advisable to consult a healthcare provider and consider alternative treatments, as melatonin is not intended as a long-term solution for sleep problems.
0- نکات ایمنی مهم درباره مصرف ایزوترتینوئین در زنان در سن باروری چیست؟: متأسفانه، داده‌های ارائه شده در منابع موجود هیچ اطلاعاتی درباره ایزوترتینوئین و نکات ایمنی مصرف آن در زنان در سن باروری ارائه نمی‌دهند. منابع موجود به موضوعات دیگری مانند درمان ناباروری با پلاسمای غنی از پلاکت، مصرف مکمل آهن و فولیک اسید در بارداری، و تراپی تستوسترون در مردان جوان می‌پردازند و هیچ اطلاعاتی درباره ایزوترتینوئین و خطرات آن برای زنان در سن باروری ندارند.
0- اسهال ناشی از آنتی‌بیوتیک‌ها را چگونه مدیریت کنیم: بر اساس تحقیقات علمی اخیر، مدیریت اسهال ناشی از آنتی‌بیوتیک‌ها عمدتاً بر استفاده از پروبیوتیک‌های خاص متمرکز است. مطالعات متاآنالیز متعدد نشان داده‌اند که پروبیوتیک‌های ویژه می‌توانند خطر اسهال مرتبط با آنتی‌بیوتیک و اسهال ناشی از کلستریدیوم دیفیسیل را کاهش دهند. این پروبیوتیک‌ها با تغییر ترکیب میکروبیوم روده، باکتری‌های مفید را افزایش داده و باکتری‌های بیماری‌زای حامل ژن‌های مقاومت آنتی‌بیوتیکی را کاهش می‌دهند. تحقیقات نشان می‌دهند که استفاده از پروبیوتیک‌ها پس از مصرف آنتی‌بیوتیک در افراد عموماً سالم با هیچ آسیب بالینی همراه نبوده است. در کودکان نیز رژیم‌های مختلف مولتی‌پروبیوتیک برای پیشگیری از عوارض فوری و تأخیری درمان آنتی‌بیوتیکی مؤثر بوده‌اند. با این حال، مدیریت مناسب آنتی‌بیوتیک‌ها همچنان برای کنترل گسترش مقاومت
0- بهترین زمان خواب برای عملکرد شناختی بهتر چیست؟: # بهترین زمان خواب برای عملکرد شناختی بهتر

تحقیقات نشان می‌دهد که خواب بین هفت تا نه ساعت در شب برای عملکرد شناختی بهینه مناسب است. مطالعات اخیر نشان داده‌اند افرادی که بیش از نه ساعت در شب می‌خوابند، عملکرد شناختی ضعیف‌تری دارند، به‌ویژه در افرادی که افسردگی دارند. همچنین، داشتن یک برنامه خواب منظم و ثابت (خوابیدن و بیدار شدن در ساعات مشخص هر روز) به تنظیم ساعت داخلی بدن کمک می‌کند و باعث بهبود تنظیم هورمون‌ها، خلق و خو، عملکرد شناختی و حتی تقویت سیستم ایمنی بدن می‌شود. خواب عمیق به‌طور خاص برای تقویت حافظه مهم است، به‌طوری که یک شب خواب خوب می‌تواند تأثیری ماندگار بر حافظه داشته باشد که حتی تا یک سال بعد نیز قابل مشاهده است.
0- آیا رژیم کیتو برای همه ایمن است؟: بر اساس اطلاعات موجود، رژیم کیتو برای همه ایمن نیست. متخصص تغذیه نیویس تأکید کرده که رژیم‌های کتوژنیک برای همه مناسب نیست و او این رژیم را به تمام مراجعان تغذیه‌ای خود توصیه نمی‌کند. با این حال، برخی از نگرانی‌های مطرح شده در مورد این رژیم، از جمله تأثیر منفی بر هورمون‌های زنان، به عنوان اسطوره معرفی شده‌اند. تحقیقات نشان می‌دهد که رژیم کتوژنیک ممکن است تقاضای هورمونی را کاهش داده و حساسیت تیروئید را افزایش دهد که نشان‌دهنده سازگاری مثبت بدن با این رژیم است. همچنین مطالعات نشان داده‌اند که این رژیم می‌تواند بهبودهای قابل توجهی در سلامت جسمی و در برخی موارد سلامت روانی ایجاد کند، اما تحقیقات در این زمینه هنوز در حال توسعه است.
0- تمرین‌های مناسب برای کمردرد خفیف کدام است: بر اساس داده‌های موجود، تمرین‌های مناسب برای کمردرد خفیف شامل تمرینات کم‌تأثیر و تقویتی است که بر روی عضلات مرکزی بدن متمرکز هستند. تمرین پل که با خوابیدن روی پشت، خم کردن زانوها به ۹۰ درجه و بالا بردن لگن تا تشکیل خط مستقیم از زانو تا شانه انجام می‌شود، برای تقویت عضلات باسن و کمر مفید است. اسکات نیز با ایستادن به عرض شانه، درگیر کردن عضلات مرکزی و پایین آوردن لگن تا موازی شدن ران‌ها با زمین، می‌تواند عضلات پایین تنه را تقویت کند. همچنین پیاده‌روی به عنوان یک تمرین کم‌تأثیر می‌تواند در کاهش عود کمردرد مؤثر باشد. این تمرینات باید با حفظ وضعیت صحیح بدن و درگیری مناسب عضلات مرکزی انجام شوند.

0- آیا ویتامین C از سرماخوردگی پیشگیری می‌کند؟: بر اساس شواهد علمی موجود، هیچ مدرک قانع‌کننده‌ای وجود ندارد که نشان دهد مصرف مکمل ویتامین C از سرماخوردگی پیشگیری می‌کند. یک بررسی در سال ۲۰۱۶ در مجله American Journal of Lifestyle Medicine نشان داد که بزرگسالانی که روزانه ۱-۲ میلی‌گرم ویتامین C مصرف می‌کردند، ۸ درصد سریع‌تر از سرماخوردگی بهبود یافتند، اما این بهبودی ممکن است به دلیل عوامل دیگری مانند استراحت و خواب بیشتر بوده باشد. در عوض، شواهد خوبی وجود دارد که نشان می‌دهد ویتامین‌های D و A از سلامت سیستم ایمنی پشتیبانی می‌کنند و مکمل ویتامین D خطر عفونت‌های تنفسی حاد را کاهش می‌دهد.
0- «تداخل SSRI با داروهای سردرد (triptans) خطر serotonin syndrome دارد؟: Based on the provided data sources, there is no specific information about the interaction between SSRIs and triptans (migraine medications) or their potential to cause serotonin syndrome. The available data mentions serotonin syndrome as a potentially life-threatening condition that can occur with certain drug combinations, specifically noting increased risk when monoamine oxidase inhibitors are used within 14 days of other serotonergic medications like fenfluramine. However, the sources do not contain any direct information about triptans or their interaction with SSRIs to adequately answer the query about this specific drug combination and serotonin syndrome risk.
0- چه زمانی درد شکمِ راست احتمال آپاندیسیت را مطرح می‌کند؟
: درد شکم راست زمانی احتمال آپاندیسیت را مطرح می‌کند که درد ابتدا از اطراف ناف یا وسط شکم شروع شده و سپس به سمت پایین راست شکم منتقل شود. این درد به تدریج طی چند ساعت شدیدتر می‌شود و با حرکت، سرفه، تنفس عمیق یا فشار دادن ناحیه بدتر می‌شود. درد آپاندیسیت معمولاً به طور ناگهانی شروع می‌شود و ممکن است فرد را از خواب بیدار کند، همچنین این درد شدید بوده و با سایر دردهای شکمی که قبلاً تجربه شده متفاوت است. اگر این درد همراه با علائمی مانند تب، تهوع، استفراغ، از دست دادن اشتها، تورم شکم یا تغییرات روده‌ای باشد، احتمال آپاندیسیت بیشتر می‌شود و نیاز به مراجعه فوری به پزشک دارد، زیرا آپاندیس می‌تواند در عرض ۴۸ تا ۷۲ ساعت پس از شروع علائم دچار پارگی شود.
0- علائم شاخص سکتهٔ مغزی که باید فوراً تشخیص داده شود کدام‌اند؟
: علائم شاخص سکتهٔ مغزی که باید فوراً تشخیص داده شود شامل افتادگی یک طرف صورت، ضعف یا فلج ناگهانی یک طرف بدن (بازو یا پا)، مشکلات گفتاری مانند تلفظ نامفهوم یا عدم توانایی در صحبت کردن، تاری دید یا از دست دادن بینایی ناگهانی در یک یا هر دو چشم، سردرد شدید و ناگهانی بدون علت مشخص، سرگیجه و از دست دادن تعادل یا هماهنگی حرکات، گیجی ناگهانی یا مشکل در درک گفتار دیگران می‌باشد. این علائم با استفاده از روش FAST قابل شناسایی هستند که شامل F (افتادگی صورت)، A (ضعف بازو)، S (مشکل گفتار) و T (زمان برای اقدام فوری) است. تشخیص سریع و درمان فوری این علائم بسیار حیاتی است زیرا هر چه زودتر درمان آغاز شود، احتمال بهبود بیشتر و عوارض کمتری خواهد بود.
0- چه زمانی در سینوزیت حاد به آنتی‌بیوتیک نیاز داریم؟

: نکات ایمنی ایزوترتینوئین در زنان در سن باروری بسیار حیاتی است زیرا این دارو یک تراتوژن قوی محسوب می‌شود و می‌تواند منجر به ناهنجاری‌های شدید و حتی کشنده در جنین شود که شامل مشکلات قلبی، مغزی و صورت است. زنان در سن باروری باید پیش از شروع درمان آزمایش بارداری انجام دهند و در طول مصرف دارو و حداقل تا یک ماه پس از قطع آن از دو روش معتبر پیشگیری از بارداری استفاده کنند. حتی یک دوز واحد ایزوترتینوئین در زمان لقاح یا دوران بارداری ممکن است باعث سقط جنین، زایمان زودرس، نقص شدید مادرزادی یا مرگ نوزاد شود. در صورت بارداری حین مصرف دارو، باید بلافاصله مصرف را قطع کرده و به پزشک مراجعه کرد. همچنین در دوران مصرف و تا یک ماه پس از قطع دارو نباید خون اهدا کرد زیرا اگر این خون به زن باردار تزریق شود، ممکن است برای جنین مشکلاتی ایجاد کند.

: استفاده از آسپیرین برای پیشگیری اولیه بیماری قلبی در افراد بدون سابقه حمله قلبی یا سکته مغزی موضوعی است که نیاز به ارزیابی دقیق دارد. گایدلاین‌های پزشکی توصیه می‌کنند که برای افراد ۵۰ تا ۵۹ ساله که تمایل به مصرف آسپیرین دارند و ریسک ۱۰ ساله حمله قلبی و سکته مغزی آنها ۱۰ درصد یا بیشتر است، این دارو می‌تواند مفید باشد. آسپیرین با رقیق کردن خون و جلوگیری از تشکیل لخته‌های خونی، خطر سکته قلبی، سکته مغزی و لخته شدن خون را کاهش می‌دهد. با این حال، تصمیم‌گیری برای مصرف آسپیرین در پیشگیری اولیه باید با در نظر گیری عوامل خطر فردی، سن، وضعیت سلامت کلی و احتمال عوارض جانبی مانند خونریزی معده انجام شود و حتماً باید تحت نظارت پزشک صورت گیرد.
0- چه زمانی زونا باید با داروی ضدویروس درمان شود؟
: زونا باید هرچه سریع‌تر با داروهای ضدویروس درمان شود، به‌ویژه در سه روز اول پس از ظاهر شدن راش‌های پوستی که در این مدت داروهای ضدویروسی تأثیر بیشتری دارند. درمان زودهنگام با داروهای ضدویروسی مانند آسیکلوویر، والاسیکلوویر یا فامسیکلوویر می‌تواند سرعت بهبودی را افزایش دهد، شدت علائم و درد را کاهش دهد، و خطر عوارض طولانی‌مدت مانند درد عصبی پس از زونا را به‌طور قابل‌توجهی کاهش دهد. این داروها معمولاً برای مدت ۷ تا ۱۰ روز تجویز می‌شوند، اما در افرادی که سیستم ایمنی ضعیف‌تری دارند مانند سالمندان ممکن است مدت درمان بیشتر از ۱۰ روز طول بکشد.
0- چه زمانی خون‌ریزی لثه نیاز به ارزیابی دندان‌پزشکی یا پزشکی دارد؟
: خونریزی لثه در برخی موارد نیاز به ارزیابی دندانپزشکی یا پزشکی دارد. اگر خونریزی هنگام مسواک زدن یا نخ دندان کشیدن مداوم باشد، می‌تواند نشانه‌ای از بیماری لثه در مراحل اولیه باشد و نیاز به بررسی دارد. همچنین اگر لثه‌ها قرمز، متورم یا در حال عقب رفتن باشند، یا اگر برآمدگی‌هایی روی لثه مشاهده شود که از بین نمی‌روند، مراجعه به دندانپزشک ضروری است. در صورتی که خونریزی شدید یا مزمن باشد و با روش‌های خانگی بهبود نیابد، حتماً باید به دندانپزشک مراجعه کرد. به طور کلی، معاینات منظم دندانپزشکی هر شش ماه یکبار برای تشخیص و درمان زودهنگام مشکلات لثه توصیه می‌شود.
0- کدام تغییرات خال پوستی (ABCDE) نیاز به ارزیابی دارد؟
: قانون ABCDE برای ارزیابی خال‌های پوستی شامل پنج معیار مهم است که هر کدام نشان‌دهنده علائم هشداردهنده‌ای هستند: A (Asymmetry) یعنی عدم تقارن که در آن یک نیمه خال با نیمه دیگر تفاوت دارد، B (Border) که به لبه‌های نامنظم، دندانه‌دار یا تار خال اشاره دارد، C (Color) یعنی رنگ غیریکنواخت که شامل رنگ‌های قهوه‌ای، سیاه، قرمز، آبی یا سفید می‌شود، D (Diameter) که به خال‌هایی با قطر بیش از ۶ میلی‌متر (به اندازه پاک‌کن انتهای مداد) اشاره دارد، و E (Evolving) که شامل هر گونه تغییر در اندازه، شکل، رنگ یا سایر ویژگی‌های خال در طول زمان است. علاوه بر این معیارها، خارش، خونریزی، زخم، پوسته‌پوسته شدن، درد یا حساسیت ناگهانی خال‌ها و همچنین ظهور خال‌های جدید در دوران بزرگسالی نیز نشانه‌های هشداردهنده‌ای هستند که نیاز به ارزیابی فوری توسط پزشک متخصص پوست دارند.
0- چه زمانی درد و تورم ساق پا می‌تواند نشانهٔ ترومبوز ورید عمقی (DVT) باشد؟
: درد و تورم ساق پا می‌تواند نشانه ترومبوز ورید عمقی (DVT) باشد زمانی که درد شدید بوده و با استراحت بهبود نیابد، همراه با تورم یک‌طرفه در ساق یا ران، قرمزی یا کبودی پوست، احساس گرما در ناحیه درگیر نسبت به سمت مقابل، و حساسیت هنگام لمس منطقه مبتلا باشد. این علائم معمولاً به‌صورت تدریجی ظاهر می‌شوند و درد هنگام ایستادن یا راه رفتن شدت می‌یابد. اگر درد ناگهانی پس از یک دوره عدم تحرک یا استراحت طولانی رخ دهد یا با مشکل در راه رفتن و تحمل وزن روی پا همراه باشد، باید فوراً به پزشک مراجعه کرد زیرا DVT یک وضعیت جدی است که در صورت جدا شدن لخته خون و حرکت آن به سمت ریه، می‌تواند منجر به آمبولی ریه و خطر مرگ شود.
0- چگونه ضدآفتاب مناسب انتخاب کنیم و اصول محافظت در برابر آفتاب چیست؟: برای انتخاب ضدآفتاب مناسب، باید به چند نکته توجه کرد. ابتدا باید از محصولی با SPF حداقل 30 استفاده کرد که 97 درصد از پرتوهای UVB را مهار می‌کند. ضدآفتاب باید طیف گسترده باشد تا در برابر اشعه UVA نیز محافظت کند. مقاومت در برابر آب نیز ویژگی مهمی است. نوع پوست در انتخاب فرمولاسیون مناسب تاثیرگذار است، پس شناخت نوع پوست ضروری است. محصولات حاوی زینک اکسید و تیتانیوم دی اکسید محافظت قوی‌تری ارائه می‌دهند. کرم‌های ضدآفتاب نسبت به اسپری‌ها پوشش بهتری دارند. علاوه بر استفاده از ضدآفتاب، باید از سایر روش‌های محافظتی مانند پوشیدن لباس مناسب و محدود کردن مواجهه با آفتاب نیز استفاده کرد.
0- چه گیاهان دارویی برای سردرد توصیه میکنی؟: برای درمان سردرد چندین گیاه دارویی مؤثر توصیه می‌شود. نعناع فلفلی یکی از بهترین گزینه‌هاست که روغن آن برای تسکین سردرد بسیار مفید است. زنجبیل نیز گیاه قدرتمندی برای کنترل سردرد و میگرن محسوب می‌شود که اثری معادل مسکن‌های شیمیایی دارد و می‌توانید آن را به صورت چای تازه یا پودر مصرف کنید. بابونه کوهی حاوی پارتنولید است که اسپاسم عضلانی را کاهش داده و از انقباض رگ‌های خونی جلوگیری می‌کند. ریحان و روغن آن برای کاهش سردرد، تنش و گرفتگی عضلات مؤثر است. سنبل‌الطیب نیز به تنهایی یا در ترکیب با گل گاوزبان به عنوان مسکن گیاهی قوی عمل می‌کند. بابونه معمولی با خواص ضدالتهابی خود نیز برای تسکین سردرد مفید است و می‌توان از آن به صورت چای گیاهی استفاده کرد.
0- چه زمانی خستگی یا ضعف طولانی‌مدت می‌تواند ناشی از سبک زندگی باشد و چه زمانی باید به بیماری‌های زمینه‌ای شک کرد؟: خستگی و ضعف طولانی‌مدت زمانی ناشی از سبک زندگی است که به دلیل خواب ناکافی، کیفیت پایین خواب، استرس مزمن، رژیم غذایی نامناسب، کمبود فعالیت بدنی یا فعالیت بیش از حد، و مواجهه با چالش‌های زندگی مانند از دست دادن عزیزان یا مراقبت از کودک جدید ایجاد شود. در این موارد معمولاً با استراحت کافی، بهبود الگوی خواب، تغذیه سالم و مدیریت استرس، علائم کاهش می‌یابد. اما زمانی باید به بیماری‌های زمینه‌ای شک کرد که خستگی مداوم و غیرقابل توضیح باشد، با استراحت بهتر نشود، بر زندگی روزمره تأثیر بگذارد، و با علائم دیگری مانند تب، کاهش وزن غیرطبیعی، درد، یا اختلال در عملکرد روزانه همراه باشد. در چنین مواردی ممکن است نشانه‌ای از کمبود ویتامین‌ها، مشکلات تیروئید، کم‌خونی، اختلالات هورمونی، افسردگی، بیماری‌های قلبی، یا سایر بیماری‌های زمینه‌ای باشد که نیاز به مراجعه به پزشک برای تشخیص دقیق و درمان مؤ
